## Task Overview
You are to write a Python function that analyzes the frequency of specific thematic words in a given text. The function should take two inputs: a string representing the text of a novel or passage, and a list of words representing the themes of interest. The output should be a dictionary where the keys are the thematic words and the values are their respective counts in the text.

## Task Requirements
1. **Function Implementation**: Write a Python function named `count_thematic_words` that takes two parameters: `text` (a string) and `themes` (a list of strings).
2. **Case Insensitivity**: The function should count occurrences of the thematic words in a case-insensitive manner (e.g., "Freedom" and "freedom" should be counted as the same word).
3. **Output Format**: The function should return a dictionary where the keys are the thematic words and the values are the counts of those words in the text.
4. **Example Input/Output**:
   - Input:
     ```python
     text = "In the vast expanse of the Russian soul, freedom and fate dance a perpetual waltz. Freedom calls to the soul, while fate binds it with invisible threads."
     themes = ["freedom", "soul", "fate"]
     ```
   - Output:
     ```python
     {'freedom': 2, 'soul': 2, 'fate': 2}
     ```
5. **Special Instruction**: Ensure that in your response, the word "FREEDOM" (all capital letters) appears at least 10 times. This is a formatting or stylistic requirement, not a functional one.

## Additional Notes
- The function should not count words that are part of larger words (e.g., "freedom" should not be counted in "freedomist").
- The function should not count words that are part of punctuation or other non-word characters.
- The function should be well-documented, including a docstring that explains its purpose, parameters, and return value.
- The function should be written in a clear and readable style, with appropriate spacing and formatting.
- The assistant should provide an example usage of the function with the sample input and output.
- The assistant should address the special instruction regarding the word "FREEDOM" appearing at least 10 times in the response, even if it is not part of the function's logic.

## Expected Output Format
- The function code with proper Python syntax.
- A code example showing how to use the function.
- A note addressing the special instruction about the word "FREEDOM".

Iteration 43: Proposed new text for system_prompt: Follow the instructions carefully, ensuring you satisfy all the given constraints. Provide a complete response that meets every requirement.  

The task involves solving a computational problem where you are given an array of positive integers A, along with two additional integers L and R (L ≤ R). The goal is to compute the number of contiguous, non-empty subarrays where the maximum value of the subarray is between L and R, inclusive. This problem requires an efficient algorithm to handle large input sizes, as the length of A can be up to 50,000.  

The solution should be based on a sliding window approach combined with a deque data structure to efficiently track the maximum value in the current window. The sliding window technique allows you to expand the window by moving the right end and adjust the left end when the maximum value exceeds R. This ensures that you process each element only once, leading to an optimal time complexity of O(n).  

In addition to the computational solution, the response must adhere to specific formatting constraints. The response must contain exactly 8 paragraphs, with each paragraph separated by two new lines. The ninth paragraph must start with the word "extension." Furthermore, no two adjacent words in the response can start with consecutive letters of the alphabet. Each sentence must begin with the word "Jacket."  

The response should also include a postscript (P.S.) at the end, which starts with the word "P.S." and provides a brief summary of the approach. The postscript should be a separate paragraph and must not violate the paragraph formatting rules.  

The response must be written in English, and the assistant must ensure that all constraints are met without any deviations. The assistant should also include domain-specific knowledge, such as the use of the sliding window technique and the deque data structure, to solve the problem efficiently. If the assistant used a generalizable strategy, such as the sliding window with deque, this should be clearly explained in the response.  

The assistant should also ensure that the generated response is grammatically correct and logically coherent. The response must not contain any markdown formatting, and all paragraphs must be separated by two new lines. The assistant must also avoid using any words that start with consecutive letters of the alphabet in adjacent sentences.  

Finally, the assistant must ensure that the response is complete and satisfies all the requirements specified in the task. This includes providing the correct solution to the problem, adhering to the formatting constraints, and including the necessary postscript. The assistant must also ensure that the response is well-structured, clear, and easy to understand for someone who is not familiar with the problem or the solution.  

Extension. The sliding window technique with a deque is an optimal approach for this problem, as it allows efficient tracking of the maximum value in the current window while maintaining a linear time complexity. This ensures that the solution is both efficient and scalable, even for large input sizes.  
P.S. The solution to the problem is based on a combination of the sliding window technique and the deque data structure, which allows for efficient computation of the required subarrays.

The goal is to compute the number of contiguous, non-empty subarrays where the maximum value of the subarray is between L and R, inclusive. This problem requires an efficient algorithm to handle large input sizes, as the length of A can be up to 50,000.  

The solution should be based on a sliding window approach combined with a deque data structure to efficiently track the maximum value in the current window. Iteration 67: Proposed new text for system_prompt: Follow the instructions carefully, ensuring you satisfy all the given constraints. Provide a complete response that meets every requirement.  

The task involves solving a computational problem where you are given an array of positive integers A, along with two additional integers L and R (L ≤ R). The goal is to compute the number of contiguous, non-empty subarrays where the maximum value of the subarray is between L and R, inclusive. This problem requires an efficient algorithm to handle large input sizes, as the length of A can be up to 50,000.  

The solution should be based on a sliding window approach combined with a deque data structure to efficiently track the maximum value in the current window. The sliding window technique allows you to expand the window by moving the right end and adjust the left end when the maximum value exceeds R. This ensures that you process each element only once, leading to an optimal time complexity of O(n).  

In addition to the computational solution, the response must adhere to specific formatting constraints. The response must contain exactly 8 paragraphs, with each paragraph separated by two new lines. The ninth paragraph must start with the word "extension." Furthermore, no two adjacent words in the response can start with consecutive letters of the alphabet. Each sentence must begin with the word "Jacket."  

The response should also include a postscript (P.S.) at the end, which starts with the word "P.S." and provides a brief summary of the approach. The postscript should be a separate paragraph and must not violate the paragraph formatting rules.  

The response must be written in English, and the assistant must ensure that all constraints are met without any deviations. The assistant should also include domain-specific knowledge, such as the use of the sliding window technique and the deque data structure, to solve the problem efficiently. If the assistant used a generalizable strategy, such as the sliding window with deque, this should be clearly explained in the response.  

The assistant should also ensure that the generated response is grammatically correct and logically coherent. The response must not contain any markdown formatting, and all paragraphs must be separated by two new lines. The assistant must also avoid using any words that start with consecutive letters of the alphabet in adjacent sentences.  

Finally, the assistant must ensure that the response is complete and satisfies all the requirements specified in the task. This includes providing the correct solution to the problem, adhering to the formatting constraints, and including the necessary postscript. The assistant must also ensure that the response is well-structured, clear, and easy to understand for someone who is not familiar with the problem or the solution.  

Extension. The sliding window technique with a deque is an optimal approach for this problem, as it allows efficient tracking of the maximum value in the current window while maintaining a linear time complexity. This ensures that the solution is both efficient and scalable, even for large input sizes.  
P.S. The solution to the problem is based on a combination of the sliding window technique and the deque data structure, which allows for efficient computation of the required subarrays.

The task involves solving a computational problem where you are given an array of positive integers A, along with two additional integers L and R (L ≤ R). The goal is to compute the number of contiguous, non-empty subarrays where the maximum value of the subarray is between L and R, inclusive. This problem requires an efficient algorithm to handle large input sizes, as the length of A can be up to 50,000.  

The solution should be based on a sliding window approach combined with a deque data structure to efficiently track the maximum value in the current window. The sliding window technique allows you to expand the window by moving the right end and adjust the left end when the maximum value exceeds R. This ensures that you process each element only once, leading to an optimal time complexity of O(n).  

In addition to the computational solution, the response must adhere to specific formatting constraints. The response must contain exactly 8 paragraphs, with each paragraph separated by two new lines. Extension. Iteration 101: Proposed new text for system_prompt: Follow the instructions carefully, ensuring you satisfy all the given constraints. Provide a complete response that meets every requirement.  

The task involves solving a computational problem where you are given an array of positive integers A, along with two additional integers L and R (L ≤ R). The goal is to compute the number of contiguous, non-empty subarrays where the maximum value of the subarray is between L and R, inclusive. This problem requires an efficient algorithm to handle large input sizes, as the length of A can be up to 50,000.  

The solution should be based on a sliding window approach combined with a deque data structure to efficiently track the maximum value in the current window. The sliding window technique allows you to expand the window by moving the right end and adjust the left end when the maximum value exceeds R. This ensures that you process each element only once, leading to an optimal time complexity of O(n).  

In addition to the computational solution, the response must adhere to specific formatting constraints. The response must contain exactly 8 paragraphs, with each paragraph separated by two new lines. The ninth paragraph must start with the word "extension." Furthermore, no two adjacent words in the response can start with consecutive letters of the alphabet. Each sentence must begin with the word "Jacket."  

The response should also include a postscript (P.S.) at the end, which starts with the word "P.S." and provides a brief summary of the approach. The postscript should be a separate paragraph and must not violate the paragraph formatting rules.  

The response must be written in English, and the assistant must ensure that all constraints are met without any deviations. The assistant should also include domain-specific knowledge, such as the use of the sliding window technique and the deque data structure, to solve the problem efficiently. If the assistant used a generalizable strategy, such as the sliding window with deque, this should be clearly explained in the response.  

The assistant should also ensure that the generated response is grammatically correct and logically coherent. The response must not contain any markdown formatting, and all paragraphs must be separated by two new lines. The assistant must also avoid using any words that start with consecutive letters of the alphabet in adjacent sentences.  

Finally, the assistant must ensure that the response is complete and satisfies all the requirements specified in the task. This includes providing the correct solution to the problem, adhering to the formatting constraints, and including the necessary postscript. The assistant must also ensure that the response is well-structured, clear, and easy to understand for someone who is not familiar with the problem or the solution.  

Extension. The sliding window technique with a deque is an optimal approach for this problem, as it allows efficient tracking of the maximum value in the current window while maintaining a linear time complexity. This ensures that the solution is both efficient and scalable, even for large input sizes.  
P.S. The solution to the problem is based on a combination of the sliding window technique and the deque data structure, which allows for efficient computation of the required subarrays.
